under the bed, in drawers and closets. I used my gift to see if there were any
thing being concealed. I found nothing in the first room.

I glanced in Kai's room and found he was being a bit more throrough. But
Emilio's handy worked was less messy. A few over turned books here and there.
But not a mess that Kai left.

When we reached the ened of the cooridor Kai had found three white sox caps.
Emilio and I had not been so fortunate. Or unfortunate, depending on how you
looked at it. But to our benefit, all of Kai's hats had been hanging on the
bunks in plain sight.

The Vega children found one hat and Kai's children had found none. It made me
feel slightly better at having found none. All the boys were detained and sent
to the office floors for interrogating. I felt bad for the boys. But it was
necessary, even I understood this. Discomfort was the few for the greater
benefit of the whole.

Their search had taken close to two hours to finish, in that time two girls were
found by some of Dae'lin's reconosense groups. There were also a baker's dozen
of adult residences that had been found with a White Sox hat in their
possessions. There was no telling how many suspects they had now, the number of
adults could vary from two per residence to upwards of six and seven depending
on the living situation. The Venatori adults liked to bunk together as they
didn't exactly stay at HQ much. You never knew who was in town and who was not.
It was going to be a mess.

The entirity of the residential search too two hours. Two hours everyone who
lived in this building had endured an invasion of their privacy. We could only
hope it bore fruit.

I was starving now. I could feel my stomach rumble, I knew others could hear it
too. But here was still work to do. Each person needed to be asked about their
wearabouts, why they had the hat, and determine if they were cesari. I could
easily do that. And I did. I looked at each person carefully.

There was about 64 people that I had to look at, but it was fairly simple to do.
I could tell from a glance that none of them where cesari. I wrote down a
persons name and their desigation by what I saw I only asked each person there
name.

I noticed that Aaron was there. He looked angry. He looked out of place and like
he should have been one of the intergogators instead of being interogated. I
smiled at him as I took in his pattern.

In addition to their name and designation I drew a simplistic pattern around
them that maybe someone else could see later. It took a lot longer than I'd have
liked. But when I was done I took my notes to Dae'lin. "This is about all I can
do to help with the interogation."

She took the paper from me and glanced at each one, "What's this? We already
know this."

I smiled. "I only asked them their name. I drew a simplistic pattern I see
around them, and what designation that tells me a person is. I'd be interested
in seeing how wrong I am. But I can't help anymore. " My stomach took that
oppurtunity to growl loudly.

Loud enough Dae'lin frowned at me. "When did you eat last?"

I laughed, "Honestly, I've not had a decent meal all day. Aaron decided my
breakfast was not good enough to eat as it landed on the floor. I had a power
bar not long ago." I shook my head, "I know, not good, I got distracted with
everything. I'll go eat now unless you need me?"

Dae'lin nodded, "You've given me your insight I think we are good. Go eat."
Dae'lin looked at her watch, "Cafeteria is done with dinner, won't be much left
I'm sure."

"Yeah I know. I'll manage. Even if that means running to the store to get food
to make."

Dae'lin laughed, "I forget you actually like cooking."

I grinned, "It's not so much as like as it's a necessity I learned to do so I
didn't have to eat in the cafeteria all the time."

Dae'lin gave me a small shove in the direction of the door. "Go eat before your
stomach chews its way out of your belly."

I laughed a I quickly snuck into the stairwell and headed towards my room. I
wondered how trashed it was.

# Caught on Fire

_Monday, June 15, 2015 10:45PM_

"Love is like a friendship caught on fire. In the beginning a flame, very
pretty, often hot and fierce, but still only light and flickering. As love grows
older, our hearts mature and our love becomes as coals, deep-burning and
unquenchable." -- Bruce Lee

I got to my room and found the door wide open and my things strewn all over the
place. How lovely. My gun was sitting out in the open left for just anyone to
come in and fire. I sighed as I put it back in the bottom of my bag. My bathroom
was trashed, all the clean white fluffy towels were laying in aheap on the
floor. Everything was mess.

I set to folding the towels. My OCD was kicking in. Dae'lin's perfection grated
on my nerves, but then again I'd become so accustomed to it I hardly noticed
when it was my training versus my own neurocies anymore.

A knock came at the door I left open. A familiar voice called out, "Nox, you
here?"

I smiled to myself, my heart started to race. I shouted from the bathroom.
"Yeah, come in to the disaster area."

Dorian walked in and stood in the doorway to the bahroom and leaned against the
frame. He watched me as I finished folding the towels and putting them in the
linen closet. "Seems my room was searched rather throughly."

Dorian laughed softly, "Mine wasn't nearly so bad. But then again I'm certain
that I was treated rather kindly due to the circumstances."

I frowned but when I looked up to see Dorian's face he was still smiling. But
the smile quickly faded and left small lines of sorry etched into his beautiful
face. Death among the Venatori was not uncommon, but this was a tragedy.

I grinned at Dorian as I leaned against the bathroom door, it gave a little
under my weight and I had to shift my feet ungraceful like. "I'm sure they were
down right nice to you."

I waved Dorian into the studio proper, there was no point standing in the
bathroom, where my mind was wandering to various things I'd like to be doing.
Things I rapidly pushed fro mmy mind. I'm starving. I need to go get something
to eat. If you don't mind coming with, we can talk on the way over, over dinner
and find someplace to finish talking about what I see."

Dorian grinned at me, "I think that will work. I know a nice little place, if
you don't mind."

I laughed, "Didn't you just come from a work dinner?"

Dorian nodded, "Yeah but the food was several hours ago. But the wine is good
and I can go for desert."

I nodded and smiled. "If that's what you want."

Dorian laughed. He looked down and saw one of my shirts that had been tossed
unceremoniously on the floor. He picked it up and chuckled to himself as he
tossed it to me. "Nice shirt."

I uncurled it from my fingers and snickered, "One of my favorites."

Dorian laughed, "I'd hit that." He said shaking his head with a wink. A lump
caught in my throat was he really suggesting what I thought he was. I swallowed
hard and tried not to show my fustration or my need.

I licked my lips and headed towards the door. "You coming?" I regretted my
choice of words the moment they were said but Dorian chuckled and followed me
out the door and closed it promptly behind him.

Dorian started for the stairs and I chuckled softly, "We can take the elavator
you know."

Dorian laughed, "Habit I suppose."

I shook my head, "You take the stairs out of habit?"

Dorian turned to me and smiled, "When I'm with you, yes." Dorian turned back to
the walk and frowned, "I didn't like the way it envoked fear in you. It's
nothing to take the stairs when I'm in your company."

"You do realized that I broke the dread of heights when I was eight years old,
at your suggestion if you recall."

Dorian nodded, "Yes, but by then I'd had it ingrained into me. Those first years
saw you in my office more times than I can count. Dae'lin having had to adjust
to you as much as you to her. I expect the same of Levi and you."

"Well if he's got as much potential as you think he does, then I'm sure we'll
butt heads a few times. How did your dinner go?"

We stopped on landing inside the stair well door. His smile was not happy more
like he was not ready to share. "I think that is something you should be sitting
for."

I laughed, "I'm not going to fall down, no matter what you say. I think I can
walk. You can't say that and not tell me now." I winked at Dorian.

Dorian sighed but continued their descent of the stairs, "The lovely lady who
Dae'lin has hired I think you might know."

"Seriously?" I shook his head, "Stella was here in the building this morning?"

Dorian nodded, "Yes. She was guaranteed the job."

Now I was confused, "Why? She didn't seem to think so."

Dorian turned a slight shade of red, it was a cute look on the tanned skinned
man. "I told her mother it was an interview, but the job was hers no matter what
if she came to interview for it."

We walked down an entire flight of stairs with their foot steps being the only
sound until Dorian continued, "This whole progeny thing threw me for a loop. To
see if I could bring myself to do what was necessary I left my station for a few
months to find someone I could try to with."

I grinned, "You mean you went to Denver to find a girl to sleep with?"

Dorian nodded, "Put bluntly, yes. I found a girl I could," Dorian's blush
deepened, "with. She was sweet and kind and young enough that my," he paused
searching for a word. I didn't interrupt I didn't realy know what he was
grasping for,. He finally continued, "inexperience wouldn't be overly weird."

"Inexperience, Dorian I seriously doubt that. With a girl maybe, but you are
hardly inexperienced."

Dorian chuckled, "And you know this, how?"

Nox could feel the blood rushing to his ears, "An educated guess."

We reached the main landing and started for the door of the stair well. Dorian
opened the door and put his hand on the small of my back and guided me through
the door a step ahead of him. I could feel a shiver run up my spine from his
touch. I had to swallow the sound that threatened to escape my mouth at his
singular touch.

Dorian fell in step with me and continued, "Well I suppose your guess is
correct, she never complained or noticed to my lack of knowledge. I stayed for
two months before I couldn't lie to her anymore. She was getting serious and I
couldn't love her." Dorian sighed, "The day I told I was leaving, she'd had
something to tell me. She insisted I go first. When I pressed her, she waved me
off but her mother sent me an email bitching me out. 'How could you leave my
daughter when she's pregnant with your child?'"

Fuck me! I closed my eyes, I couldn't imagine that feeling, not really though I
imagined it was painful. I didn't have to ask how it happened because Dorian
answered my unspoken question, "She'd been sick, the condom broke, antibotic and
that screwed us pretty good. We thought things were okay. But apparently not.
I'd told her mother I didn't love her daughter, but I would help however
necessary, through her. She agreed. Stella lost her job about a week ago. When
she told me Stella lost her job, I arranged for Dae'lin to hire her."

"Dae'lin's assistant's time was ending anyway, and with Stella, Dae'lin won't
need to replace her for a while. The meeting last night was informing Stella
that her son was different."

I nodded, "And that you were different. And she was about to become venatori."

Dorian nodded, "Yes. Her son is likely Magnus. 100% of minorem born to a human
mother that both mother and child have surived have been Magnus."

"I know the statistic."

Dorian smiled, "I firgured you would. You did quite a bit of research on your
past if I recall."

"Only on that, not curious enough to find out who my father was." I gave a
hesitant laugh, I really hadn't cared back them to find out who my father was.

Dorian nodded, "Yes, there is that. If I'd known you'd met Stella, I wouldn't
have made the suggestion for yesterday."

I frowned, "Why not? You expected me to sleep with her?"

Dorian laughed, "Actually yes. I didn't expect the child to inhibit your natural
inclination."

Nox smiled, "Seems I still have a few surprises left."

"You do at that." Dorian lead the way through the large double doors of the
building and headed for the subway platform around the corner. We didn't chat
much while we caught the D train heading towards Little Italy. Despite the hour
it was relatively full car, it seemed everyone piled into this one car. There
was standing room only. Which wasn't a bother really.

Dorian chose a spot near the rear of the car and used the strap to keep his
balance. I reached up just as the car lurched to a start and held on to the same
one. The motion of the car pressing Dorian's hip into the front of me. We were
close enough to whisper, I could feel Dorian's breath on my cheek before he
spoke, "I didn't plan this honest."

I laughed softly, "I wouldn't have minded if you had." I really wouldn't have, I
could feel his body heat through my hoodie and jeans and I wanted to touch the
man next to me. I really needed to get this crap out of my system somehow.

We didn't talk the entire trip on the train. We looked at each other with
smiles, pressed against one another until we reached our destination. 15 minutes
later I was nearly breathless from his touch. Dorian grinned as I slid my hand
into his and entwined our fingers together. We held hands to the turn stiles,
how that one little moment had changed things.

The air outside felt crips and cool compared the to stuffy heated air of the
underground subway system. Dorian headed towards Mulberry Stree and wrapped his
arm around my waist. My heart skipped a beat. Dorian was being touchy ad that
was so very not Dorian. I had known Dorian for years, and I'd only seen him once
with another man, and I was in a restricted area and he had been kissing the
man. The thought stirred parts of my body and I tried to redirect my thoughts.

They rounded the corner there were any number of food joints on Mulberry Street,
it was after all Little Italy, for which I was actually grateful for, it was one
thing I'd missed when I was out west. I could get great Mexican food, but
Italian, not so much.

We past several little places that would have suited my tastes just fine, but
when we stopped in front of the would-be maroon awning of Pellegrino's I was
surprised. Dorian had fine tastes, but it was a bit too fine for my pay check.
But I didn't object when Dorian opened the door for me, I should have said
something. I felt as Dorian's hand slide along the small of my back as I walked
in front of the other man. Such a small gesture and I was melting already at his
touch. This was going to be an interesting night.

The hostest greet Dorian with surprise, "Didn't you just leave?"

Dorian laughed, "My friend is hungry, I figured I could use another bottle of
wine and keep him company."

She smiled, "Right this way Mr. Vega."

The woman lead us to a table, they were almost at capacity even this late at
night. It was a wonder that the city that never sleeps really was like this even
this late at night. I would have to readjust my expectations of life again if I
intended to stay in the City.

We sat down and the woman left menus with us. Dorian picked up the wine menu,
"You have any preferences?"

I laughed, "I'll trust your judgement, I'm more a beer kinda guy."

Dorian smiled, "We can go elsewhere." He was being curteous to me? He didn't ask
when we walked in here, and I really couldn't complain though I should.

I shook my head, "Here is fine. I missed good Italian food." I opened the menu
and started browsing and I tried not to react the prices on the menu. But I knew
I'd be working this meal off in many ways. It wasn't uncommon to spend more than
I'd like on a date, but this wasn't exactly a date either.

Our waitor came to the table, "I am Miguel, I will be your server today. Can I
start you off with anything?"

Dorian spoke calmly, "We'll have a bottle of Sauvignon Blanc. I'll poke at his
plate while I wait for desert." He smiled at me and I couldn't help but laugh.

"You think I'm sharing?" I grinned playfully at Dorian.

Miguel smiled and looked tome expectantly, "Are you ready to order?"

I smiled up at him with my best smile, "Yeah, I'll start off with Mozzarella
Della Casa."

"And your meal?" He asked with a slight frown. Not one to flirt with, I dialed
back

"Pollo Pastore." I ordered with a little less flair which earned me a smile from
Miguel and from Dorian.

Dorian nodded approvingly at my choices when Miguel left Dorian smiled,
"Couldn't have done better myself."

I beamed, "Ain't my first rodeo. Though I do hope they bring something quickly,
I'm starving."

Dorian asked, "You forget to eat today?"

"Something like that. Just busy I didn't think about it until I went looking for
Kai with your father." I sighed, "He's a power horse. I don't think I could have
picked up directly after my loved one died. Not like he did."

Dorian sighed, "He will power through it until it's over and then he'll crash. I
think we all will. None of us have felt the pain yet, I know I haven't." Dorian
paused and put a litle thought into his words, "How did you manage, when you
lost your mother?" Almost like he didn't know how to ask the question he had.

I shrugged, "I wasn't close to my mother. I got through it with relatively
little pain. I only have guilt for the circumstances really. If I'd done my job
properly, if I'd not let her superior old school philosphy overrule my
judgement. If Jace were to go, or Dae'lin or even you, that would be something
else entirely. My family is not one of blood."

Dorian smiled, "I'm family?"

I laughed, "Closest I've come to it anyway."

Dorian sighed, "That doesn't bode well for this..." He waved his hand over the
table, "Whatever this is."

I grinned, "And there is doubt to what this is?" I winked at Dorian, it was
meant to display the humor and the suggestive nature of my comment, and Dorian
played right along.

"You have none?" Dorian asked a smile playing on his face.

"The night is still young." Miguel arrived with a basket of freshly baked bread
and I could see the steam rolling off the top and the patterns above the bread
were playing havoc on others around it, it was all sort of harmonious. My mouth
started to water. I looked up at Migued, "You are a god." I winiked at Dorian
and took a peice of bread before it even hit the table. I didn't even bother
with buttering it.

Dorian chuckled, "Don't mind my friend here, he's been starving himself all day
just to fit into those lovely jeans of his."

I laughed, nearly chocking on the bread I had just bitten into. The waitor left
in a hurry as if he'd gotten more than he bargained for at our table, he
probably had.

I finished chewing, "You scared him away." I winked at Dorian, "So my jeans..."
I left it hanging on purpose and watched the scarlet color rise in Dorian's
cheeks before he took a sip of his water. I grinned and took another bite of the
warm peice of bread.

I swallowed and change the topic, "Do you see the patterns around the bread?"

Dorian adjusted in his chair, the interest in the topic peaking his curiousity
in a way that flirting hadn't, I smiled at the fact, but I also wondered if I
was still reading way too much into the whole situation. Dorian strained, I
could tell he was focusing intently on the cooling bread, he finally nodded,
"Yeah, they look like they are dissipating though."

I nodded, "They are cooling down. That's how it looks around people, except it
oscillates, Kai who bends fire and earth, he'll oscillate pretty steadily
between attracking fire and earth. Indicating he actually is as strong in both."

I paused to think about the patterns I'd seen today. I had noticed alot of
changes, the most notable was in Jason, "Jason. He's changed a little since I
was here last. He is strong in Air and earth, but he's got a little fire and a
small oscilation of water now too."

Dorian nodded, "You should sit in his class one day and listen to him speak. I
won't do his theory justice, but it's pretty simple. If you can train your eye
to see the patterns, you can manipulate them all to some degree or another. You
inspired him."

I smiled, "So that means you can manipulate all the elements?"

Dorian shrugged, "Can't teach an old dogs new tricks."

Nox laughed, "I bet I could teach you a few new tricks." I winked at Dorian. He
blushed slightly and I knew my comment had hit the intended mark. The thought
made my body stir and my heart flutter faster. I was at least enjoying the
company and the flirting. "You've seen them far longer than anyone else and say
you can only just touch Air. I think you are your own interferrance."

Dorian smiled, "Perhaps, but I will stick to my guns."

"You are no fun." I pouted playfully.

# Best Sleep Ever

_Monday, June 15, 2015 11:15PM_

Migues brought out the anti-pasto I had ordered. He set the plate down in the
middle of the table and placed a plate in front of each of us. Dorian nodded to
him in thanks. The fresh buffalo and smoked mozzarella, tomato, roasted peppers
and basil looked to die for, almost too pretty to eat. I didn't waste much time
taking a bit of the dish to my plate.

A second waitor came bearing gifts, well not really, the wine was presented to
Dorian and he nodded, the server poured two glasses and Dorian took small sip
and savored it. I watched Dorian test the wine to his satisfaction. The man left
the bottle sitting on the table. I took a sip of the wine, i'd never been a fan
of wine, but it was fruity and I smiled. I couldn't say much more about the
wine.

My stomach took that moment to growl and I looked to Dorian witha smile. "I'm
tarving." Dorian gave me a smile as I popped a bit into my mouth. The first bite
was exuqisite and I was drooling. I could have done my Homer impression but not

# Connections

_Tuesday, June 16, 2015 9:30AM_

I was half way to my rooms when I caught the distinct sight of a small gym. I
stopped outside the propped open door and peired inside. I could use a short
work out, vent some of my fustration. My neck was a little sore from sleeping on
the couch. I was surprised my back wasn't sore too. I smiled at the memories of
what little dreams I remembered having. I remembered the scents most, but that
had been Dorian's pillow. I rubbed the back of my neck out of reflex.

A voice from behind me made me jump, "Rough night?"

I turned around and saw my father smirking at me. He was carrying a bunch of
files, a towel and a bottle of water. He was dressed to work out. He looked like
he was going to work and work out at the same time. I had done it many times,
apparently it ran in the family.

I grinned at him, "Sleeping on the couch does that." I stepped away from the
door but Kai stood where he was. He looked at me like he knew where I was and he
thought I was lying.

"While youa re here." Kai handed me the files he'd been arying and he went
inside putting the rest of his things on the bench as he started warming up with

I took a look at the files and noticed that these were the same files I had been
working. I looked down at my father stretching and he just shrugged. He didn't
bother explaining why he'd taken my work.

"These are Dorian's files on Cesari and me and others like me. They are how he
came to his theory. These files are from Mrs. Vega about the two cases of yours
and Emilio that could possibly fit Dorian's theory. But since none of them can
bend all the elements only thing I can figure is it's Exuli helping out. It
would fit with Dorian's theory."

"I haven't had time to go through the files yet as the fire alarms went off, and
then we went on a scavenger hunt for the baseball hats."

Kai had moved from stretches to shadow boxing. I watched him as he moved
flawlessly from form to form. He moved with precision and speed I was envious
of. I could have the precision, but the speed not so much. "What are these two
cases you think are connected?"

"They are two exiles you were party to. One was a woman whom you carried out
kicking and screaming. The other you excorted calmly to Texas."

Kai nodded. "Okay. But none of them are Magnus."

I nodded my head in confirmation, "Correct."

"Where are they located?"

I looked through their files. "Mrs. Cox hasn't checked in for about 30 years.
She was last in Chicago with a daughter and her son was exiled with her. The
others checked in two months ago still in Africa where they fled to." I smirked,
"Preaching the word of God!"

Kai laughed, "How ironic. Looks like Chicago is our link."

I nodded. "Seems to be a good start."

Kai took the papers from my hands and set them down on the bench, "You came here
for a reason?"

I smirked, "I was doing that when you rudely took the files away."

Kai laughed and shook his head, "I meant the here and now. Outside the gym." He
still looked like he thought I was lying about sleeping on the couch.

"I guess. I was debating it." I sighed, "Haven't had a good workout in a few

Kai smiled at me, "Show me what ou got boy."

I'd like to watch you work all the elments like that."

once we catch this guy."

Kai smiled and headed for the door with his bottle of water and his towel around
his shoulders. "Let me know what you find in the files. I'll leave it to you
since you have a handle on the theory. I will be questioning our inside man
suspects again today.

I sighed. My father was gone just as fast as he had come into my morning. I was
left with the need to shower even more than before, but I'd found a bit more

"I can do better than that." I smiled from ear to ear, "Dorian I'd like to cook
dinner for you tonight, would that be acceptable?" I felt nervous, I don't know
if I could handle it if he said no right now. My heart sank at my own thoughts.

"Well I suppose I can make th time to watch you dance around my kitchen some
more."

I laughed, "Who said was cooking in your apartment?"

"I..." Dorian sounded hurt.

I interrupted before Dorian could continue, "Dorian I'd love to cook for you at
your place."

"Would you like me to pick anything up?"

I sighed, "Everything. Steak, salad fixing, whatever you like. The wine?"

Dorian laughed, "You aren't going to surprise me?"

I grinned, "I think you've had enough of my surprises. I can pick it up if I
find the time don't worry about it."

"Like you ate yesterday, nah, I'll do it. I'll send someone to get it." There
was a comfortable silence over the phone and I sighed with contentment, Dorian
laughed, "I've never had anyone want to cook for me."

I grinned, "Good, I'll see you tonight, 7 sound good."

Dorian chuckled, "Sure thing. I'll see you later. But a date wasn't what I was
calling about. You saw your father this morning?"

I nodded knowing Dorian couldn't see it, "Yeah, you hear everything don't you?"

Dorian chuckled, "He stopped in my office to congradulate me on a job well done.
He mentioned your theory on the Exuli, claimed it was all my idea. I nodded and
shook his hand and had no clue what he was on about. You can enlighten me at
dinner about that encounter as well. He never once called you boy either."

"He said he wouldn't, I'm impressed. It was a good morning." I grinned, "A very
good morning everything including waking up on the couch in your living room."

"Happy to oblige. I look forward to seeing you later." Dorian hung up the phone
and my heart was fluttering with excitement. I was surprised at the reaction so
quickly. I walked into the bathroom and started the shower just as a knock
sounded at his door. "Oy."

I turned off the water and walked out to the front door. I was never going to
get a shower. I opened the door and Levi pushed his way inside, "Can I show you
something?"

"Be my guest." I was glad he'd come to me, and more importantly I was glad he
was practicing.

He looked around and laughed, "This is a boring room. So not what I expected."

I laughed too, "It is and it's only temporary."

Levi nodded and sat down on the edge of my bed. He put his hands in front of
him, "I've been practicing. I know I'm not supposed to but..."

In one hand Levi held a small smooth stone. Leavi mporphed the pattern in his
other hand to recreate the rock perfectly. I was impressed, it wasn't just a
replica it was identical down to the life sparks inside. I grinned at Levi, "
Well done."

I created a simple singular flame in my hand, "And this?"

Levi held his hand out and replicated the dancing flame without a flaw. He
struggled a little but he saw the patterns, "You see the patterns?"

Levi nodded, "I always have. Ijust didn't understand. I thought I was seeing
things. But when I listened to those kids described what they saw you do. I was
like, I see that. I see you differently, you move differently. Different than
Mr. Hill or Dorian or any of my other instructors."

I laughed, "That's because I'm Cesari. You do the same thing."

Levi nodded, "I have a class to get to. Can we talk later?"

I nodded, "Sure aytime before 7, I have plans after that."

Levi nodded, "Alright." And just as he had arrived Levi was gone out of my
bedroom door. My mood was elevated again. I glanced at the shower and shrugged.
I was never going to get a shower so I changed my shirt and picked up the files
and headed to the Archives to do my research that Kai had approved. I guess I
had work to do now.

# Family

_Tuesday, June 16, 2015 11:00AM_

I started down to the archives with a clean shirt on, it was tame by my
standards, and hopefully to those in the archives too. My hoodie was unzipped
but I could zip it if necessary. But my walk got interrupted by a phone called.
"Hello?" I hoped it was Dorian but the small voice that answered had me
frowning.

"Yeah Nate, I'll be right down." My data was ready for me, he'd gotten to it
sooner than I'd expected. Instead of stopping at the Archives floor I headed
down to the basement and Nate's "bat cave"

Nate was hunkered down behind his desk while a familiar frame stood in front of
him. I wasn't exactly sure if I was happy or scared to see my father. I wasn't a
praying man, but I hoped my father was in a better mood.

The kid looked up at me and frowned as he saw me in the doorway. Kai turned
around and smiled, "Fancy meeting you here."

I grinned at my father in hopes to disarm him. "I just came to get the data from
my destroyed laptop."

Nate quickly handed me the jump drive he'd put the data on and cleared his
throat nervously, "I just copied the documents, movies, pictures and music,
nothing else." The boy was clearly nervous. He turned a nice shade of red as he
remembered what I'd said I had on my harddrive. I laughed to myself.

Kai turned around to see the boy blushng and the red deepened, "What's that all
about?" He asked me as he turned around.

I laughed, "I told him I had porn, girls I filmed on there." Kai's eyes
narrowed, "I swear there was nothing on there. I told him so."

Nate started spuluttering. I chuckled, "I'm sorry dude. It was a joke."

Kai shook his head, "You like to step in it don't you?"

I grinned, "The more the better. It keeps people guessing. And I don't look
foolish when others try to make me look like a fool. I do a damned fine job of
it."

Kai nodded for me to follow him out. He turned to Nate, "Keep up the good work
and thanks for tht bit of tech help. It's greatly appreciated."

Nate nodded and beamed with pride as his grandfather praised him. I could see
how it could make one smile. Kai started out the door, "You were done?"

I held up my flash drive, "Just getting my harddrive."

We walked in silence for a while. Kai interrupted it, "So... Dorian?"

I looked at him with a questioning look. He smiled at me, "I'm not stupid.
Rumors run around here like wild fire. And I happened to see you leaving his
room this morning before stopping at the gym door."

I sighed, "Nothing happened."

Kai gave me a perplexed look. "Why not?"

"I don't kiss and tell Kai." I laughed, "But since when did you become
interested in my sex life?" I didn't expect an answer it didn't really matter.

Kai answered anyway. "Since the wife of my best friend died."

I nodded, "Death does that. But why do you care now? I'm still everything you
hate about me."

Kai frowned. "Hate is a very strong word." There was silence as they ascended
the stairs. "They don't need more problems Nox." I made to protest that I wasn't
going to cause problems, but Kai held up his hand, "Let me finish first. I know
you don't intend to cause problems. But they tend to follow you around. Dorian
is in a fragile state."

I had to interrupt, "That's the very reason WHY nothing happened. I'm not stupid
or uncaring and I sure as hell don't want to hurt Dorian. I LIKE Dorian."

Kai nodded, "And I don't want you to get hurt either." There was sadness in
Kai's voice, "But that it isn't the whole truth. Dae'lin told me what happened
to you as a child."

"Fuck!" I could feel the anger rising, Dae'lin couldn't keep her damned mouth
shut. "It doesn't matter, there is nothing you can do about it now."

Kai sighed, "There was and I did."

I stopped without thinking where I was. I could feel the fear and the pain and
everything that Garret had ever inflicted up on me. I could see him in my minds
eye coming after me. I could feel him beating me again. I whispered, "What did
you do?"

Kai took a few steps back down as he'd climbed a few stairs after I'd stopped.
He looked at me in my state of panic and he put his hand on my arm, "He was
exiled. Dae'lin stopped me from doing what I intended to do." Kai's anger was
written all over his face. "You and I may not get along Nox. But you ARE my
blood, and no one treats my blood the way Garret treated you."

I stood paralyzed with fear. Garrett would know I told, would know I caved. I
swallowed hard, I felt like I was five again. Kai stared at me "You aren't alone
anymore."

I shook my head and whispered, "You shouldn't have done that."

Kai looked lost, even more lost than I felt. I sank to the stair my feet were on
and turned to sit. I couldn't move, I couldn't breathe. Garrett...

Kai sat with me. He asked in a quiet voice, "Do I need to call someone?"

I shook my head. I would be fine. I had to calm myself down. I took a deep
breath and pushed away the fear. It was the only thing I could do. The ache in
my back persisted, the phantom strikes always lingered. I could still see them
in my head, but I ignored them. I stood up and whispered, "You should have
killed him."

I started up the stairs and when Kai caught up he grabbed my arm and out of
habit I pulled it from his grasp. I yelped, "Please don't touch me right now."

Kai raised an eyebrow, "Is it that bad kid?"

I turned to look at my father, "You have no idea how bad it gets." I sighed, "I
wish Dae'lin hadn't told you. She can't keep her damn mouth shut."

Kai shook his head, "She cares, that's all."

My voice was quiet and distant, "She only wants to do her duty. Garrett did his
job. He did his duty." I spat out the words, "I don't spark out of fear. I don't
spark out of anger." I leaned in and my voice grew dark, "He beat the spark out
of my flesh. I learned control. I am who I am because of him. He did his duty
too." I stalked off.

Now I was pissed. But I'd take that over afraid, anything but afraid. I wasn't
some five year old kid to be pushed around. My father caught up to me again this
time he didn't try to touch me. "Talk to me Nox. What can I do?"

I stopped. "Kai. There is nothing you can do. You can't go back in time and
change things. You can't protect me from myself. It's something **I** have
to do for myself. Even if you could go change it, I don't want you to. I am me
because of him. I don't hide behind the fact that he beat me Kai. I told no one.
Am I damaged from it? Yes. Am I broken? Yes. But I am me. I won't change me
cause you think I deserve pity. I like who I am. It took years upon years of
talking with Margo about it, but I'm okay with me now." I sighed. "You want to
help?"

Kai nodded. I took a step back, cleared the space between us, "Talk to Margo,
figure out how you can fit into my mental health plan and goals. I'll set you an
appointment. You can talk with her. You are part of my issues despite not even
having known me. I will let you in, let you help but I don't know how Kai. My
default mode is to push you away. To make you angry so I don't have to be hurt
again."

Kai snickered, "For being someone who pushes away you are open about all of it."

I grinned, "You caught me in an off moment. Instead of internalizing my shit you
got to hear it. This is my life, Kai. I fight panic attacks every day. I wake
myself up with nightmares every night. I don't sleep out of fear of my dreams. I
push people away so they don't hurt me. These are the tip of the iceberg. And
yet no one knows half of it."

Kai frowned, "And now Dae'lin has voided your trust of her?"

I nodded, "Yes. Just in time for the fucking breeding program negotiations."

Kai sighed, "I will see to it that your demands are met, and I will impinge a
few additional on them."

"Why would you do that?"

Kai grinned, "Because I'm your father and they owe me a few favors. Don't
concern yourself with them." Kai put his arm around me tenatively and when I
didn't shrug him off he pulled me close. "I ask only one thing of you. I want to
know my grandkids like I didn't get to know you."

I smiled, "Of course."

Kai nodded in the direction of the doors we were about the pass, "This is me.
Nox..." He waited until I looked at him. "Let me know when I should go see your
therapist."

I nodded, "I'll text you the details." Kai nodded and headed onto the floor he
had left me on. I started my way up to the Archives, I would finally get some
work done.

# It Changes Everything

_Tuesday, June 16, 2015 11:30AM_

I finally made it back to the Archives, it was nearly noon and I hadn't made any
progress on what Kai asked me to look into. But that was hardly my fault. But
before I started I figured it was a good time to call Margo's assistant and set
up a time for her and my father to meet.

I dialed her number without looking up the contact. I called her that often
before there was such a thing as a cell phone. I wasn't even as old, I'd had a
cell phone since I was in my early teens. But I called Margo more as a child
then I did now. And I still called her regularly.

I called her direct line, but it apparently forwarded to Megan's desk. The
chipper voice answered. "Dr. Silverman's office, how can I help you?"

I grinned, "Hey Megan. Margo's busy?"

Megan laughed, "A big client is in a three hour session. She is not to be
disturbed."

"That's fine, I need to set up an appointment for my father to sit down with her
and chat about me and how he can _fit_ into things."

I could hear Megan tapping away at the keyboard. "She's got an hour next week
Wednesday for a lunch discussion, since I assume he's not here to talk to her
about his issues."

I laughed, "Not to my knowledge. Can you have the paperwork ready when I get in
next week so she can legally let him see my file? He'll ask, he's as anal about
things as Dorian and Dae'lin."

Megan tapped away at her keyboard again, "I can. It also looks like you need to
update your permission for that all around. Who else should have access so I can
set that paperwork up?"

I thought about it. There was no reason for anyone to ever need to look at my
files except me again. I wasn't a minor. But ... habits, "Just my father and
Dorian." Dae'lin lost the rights when she told my secrets to someone else.

I could hear Megan smile, "Alright Nox, I've got that taken care of. Next
Wednesday, Jun 24th at 12pm, Dr. Silverman will see your father. Would you like
me to send you a reminder for your calendar?"

"Yeah, I can forward that to Kai."

"I will send it to him as well, to save you the trouble. Is there anything else
I can do for you?"

"Nope, my standing appointment is booked still?"

Megan laughed, "You know very well that Margo would not overbook that slot.
You've been seeing her every Monday at 9:30 for 16 years. It's penciled in until
the end of time."

I grinned, "Just making sure. I'll see you then." And then I hung up the phone
and sighed, it was time to actually get back to work.

I got back to work with that taken care of. It was nothing that had to be done
right then, but I'd likely forget and I'd hate to disappoint my father. And I
really was procrastinating. I had to do research, the most dull of things a
venatori hunter can do. But it was necessary.

I pulled the large book of Exuli towards me and wished I had my laptop to access
the digital records. I could hunt down a free to use one but that would waste
time I could be doing this.

Thankfully there were books for indexing and I was able to find all the Exuli
currently living in Chicago. There were five families - including Levi's. It was
a small fact that I had forgotten and that nagging feeling like I'd missed
something stopped. It was the missing peice. and that meant I had to go find
Levi.

I grabbed all of their files and set out to Dae'lin's office to have someone
track down their whereabouts, but I didn't really think it was necessary. But it
was Dae'lin's or Gary's job to do this and Dae'lin was just easier.

The annoying ring tone of an unknown caller swept through the stair well. I was
getting tired of not having people in my contacts, I was going to have to fix
that. I answered, "Yeah?"

"Nox? Have you heard?" A familiar voice sounded on the verge of anger and
concern yet I couldn't place the voice.

I shrugged as I continued my ascent to Dae'lin's office, "Heard what?"

"Your father..."

I interrupted, "What about my father? I just saw him."

"He's...", a short distance from the phone the voice called out. "Dorian. Good.
I've got Nox now. Make sure everyone else makes it up here."

I could hear Dorian's very patient and quiet voice that signaled he was tired of
hearing the same things, or repeating himself, "I know Father. You told me
already."

I at least now knew who it was on the other end of the phone, "What happened
Emilio?" I was getting concerned now.

Emilio let out an exasperated huff of air, "Kai has been stabbed."

"What?" It was more shock than anything, "I just saw him. How?" I had just seen
him, I glanced at the time on my phone, it was maybe 30 minutes ago.

Emilio sounded distant and like he was trying to keep his anger at bay, "He was
found in a pool of his own blood. I'm on my way to find the culprit on the
cameras. Same security room we were in last time. Meet me there."

It was hard to fathom how this could happen inside headquarters, there
definitely was an inside man, and I had a pretty good idea who it was now -
there was no such thing as coincidence! I had to find Levi. I told Emilio, "I
have to do something first. I'll be there in a bit."

Emilio nearly yelled, "Nox, this is important! Kai is in surgury, we have to
find this man. He's taking everything from us. You have to help me." He was
sounding more and more desparate, and I didn't blame him, but what I had to do
was just as important.

I took a deep breath, "Trust me. What I have to do is important too. We might be
able to use what I find to help in that search. Please Emilio I have to."

Emilio sighed, "Fine!" And he hung up. I felt bad, but my gut said to find Levi.
I had to follow my hunch.

But this was bad news. How had Kai gotten taken by surprise? That could be the
only explanation. I leaned against the wall in a daze. I was having a hard time
collecting my thoughts, and it was only the sounds of lockdown that brought me
around to the task at hand.

Lockdown would give me problems getting around, but that also meant everyone
else would have problems too. There were ways around the compound without
security on your side, but that was known to only a few, and I wasn't one of
them.

I called Emilio back. He answered with a gruff, "What?"

I sighed, he was angry at me, or maybe just angry in general, it didn't matter
realy though I did feel bad he thought I was ignoring my father. "Lockdown your
idea?"

Emilio spoke quickly, "No from down upon high."

I nodded, I was surprised it hadn't been done the moment Kai was found. I guess
it took a while to get that high up. "I need some assistance with lockdown."

Emilio sighed, "What are you doing, Nox?"

I grinned, "I think a kid I'm mentoring is involved. I don't want to say
anything too loudly just in case he's not, but I don't beleive in coinisidence
and there are too many in this siutation to beleive otherwise."

"Go on."

"He's cesari. He's from Chicago. I know he's new, he's a boy, and he fits the
only description Nick gave of him. I vaguely remember him wearing a sox hat the
day I met him."

"What do you need from me?" Emilio sounded hopeful.

"I'm heading to the boy's dormintory to look for him. I can't get there alone
with a lockdown."

I walked through the cooridors with caution, there was a murderer about. And I
didn't fancy getting stabbed. I didn't have a pattern at the ready, but I didn't
really need to. The boy's dormintory was two floors from my current position. I
just needed to take the stairs. Emilio followed me on the cameras, I could
almost feel his eyes on me. It was unnerving.

I could hear the senior Vega's breathe over the phone, it was ragged and
strained, he was worried. "He'll be okay."

"What?" Emilio asked?.

I smiled, "My Dad, he'll be okay. He's a tough son of a bitch. A knife won't be
what takes him down."

Emilio laughed, "You are probably right, but we need to find this bastard, and
if you think that kid has something to do with it. Then we better find him. The
stairs ahead are unlocked. You can go up to the boys dorms."

I nodded at the next camera in thanks. The stairs cameras had blind spots it was
too expensive to monitor every nook of the wells but it wasn't possible to move
in the stairs without being seen. I trusted Emilio to tell me if he saw anything
I needed to worry about.

I wanted to take the stairs two at a time but I controlled my pace I knew what
could happen. I finally got up the two floors and Emilio opened the door for me
and I walked into the common area of the boy's dormintory. There were a group of
small boys who crying in the corner. My heart went out to them. I walked slowly
over to their huddled forms and knelt down. "It's alright. No one is goig to
hurt you."

One of the litle boys had the olive skin and golden locks. Nox vaguely
remembered him, but he couldn't remember why. His golden eyes blinked at him and
it was the only thing Nox needed to remember, he was the half dragon boy.
"Drake, right?"

He looked up at me with tears in his eyes and then he wrapped his arms around me
and hugged me tightly around the neck. I hugged him back, "Drake, it'll be okay.
I promise." I could feel the boy take a deep breath against my neck, and I knew
what he was doing. I remembered doing the same thing when I was five years old.

The elevator had been fine in the basement. It wasn't until Dorian and I were
riding up past the lobby that I saw how high we were and the fear took over. I
grabbed on to the demin of Dorian's faded blue jeans and I held on to him and
took in his scent. It was the first time I'd felt safe since leaving my home. I
closed my eyes and I could smell the cinamon and vanilla and the light musk of
Dorian almost as if he were here. I whispered to Drake, "What do you smell?" I'd
never asked anyone before.

Drake whispered back, "You smell like a campfire - like home."

I grinned over his shoulder, "Do you trust me?"

I could feel the boy nod against my neck. "Okay." I set the boy down and held
him out from me and lookd at him and the three other boys. "Drake. I need you to
take these other boys to he orange door around the corner. I want you four to
stay there until I come back. Do you understand me?"

Drake nodded. "I will be back when it's safe." As the boys left the other side
door opened and Mr. Lance came out. "Mr Lance. Can you show me to Levi Hughes
room?"

Mr. Lance nodded and headed down one of he halls. "Is he the reason for lock
down?"

I shook my head, "No sir. My father was stabbed. Though I think he's involved
and could be dangerous."

Mr. Lance unlocked the door and there was no one there, it was empty. "He's
alone?"

"Yes, his mentors didn't think he was suited for company yet."

I shook my head "That didn't help either." I sighed, "Thank you. Get to safety
and there are four boys in the fire room that was empty. I will be back to get
them out. I don't expect them to open the door for anyone but me."

Mr Lance nodded, "Alright. I understand." I patted the man on the shoulder and
headed back to the common room.

# Finding Levi

_Tuesday, June 16, 2015 12:40PM_

It was difficult to say where Levi might go. I called Emilio. "Yes Nox."

"Levi's not in his rooms."

Emilio sighed, "I'll do a sweep through the cameras, we should have face
recognition on him I will let you know when I have him. I've seen the man who
stabbed your father. I don't have a clear picture yet, but when I have that
everyone will get that message."

"Good. I'll start searching through the cooridors from here as if I were looking
for a place to hide."

"Sounds good. You should see your family soon. Comfort them."

I sighed, "They aren't my family."

"They are boy, you and they just need to be reminded of that. See your father,
Nox."

I nodded, "Yes, sir, I will when this is done."

"I will accept that. I will call when this is done." Emilio hung up and I
started out the double doors and looked down either end of the hall. Where would
I go if I wanted to get away?

To the left was the cafeteria. To the right nothing much but storage and
classrooms and the like. I went right. The cafeteria would have people and I'd
be looking to avoid as many as I could.

I walked slowly checking each door to see if they were locked. It was slow and
meticulous but it was better than hunting in the forest. I wasn't sweating my
ass off or freezing my toes with wet and cold. He could be in any of the locked
rooms but it was unlikely.

I found a room that was unlocked it was marked storage. I walled off the section
of the with patterns of air to make sure no one followed me. I set down a guide
for Emilio if he came looking for me and put my phone on silent.

I put a wall of air on the door too just in case I wasn't alone inside. I used a
small globe of fire and air to see by, it gave off an orange flickering light
that reminded me of a campfire. It was oddly comforting.

The room was lined with shelves and there were additional rows of metal shelves.
There were boxes of things and some solitary items sitting on the shelves. I
remained quiet, I could call out his name, but I had decided that the light was
more than enough, he wasn't getting away.

I went down one row, one foot in front of the other, slow and steady as I'd been
taught to hunt all manner of beast. I never expected to hunt another like me - a
cesari or even a Venatori.

I didn't like this. I didn't like hunting human or Venatori. I didn't want to
hurt another again. I knew I'd have to one day, again. In defense of my own life
or those I care about. But I didn't want to have to put down someone. I crept
through the aisles. I wanted to be else where.

I could feel the air move around me. I could sense that someone was in here with
me. They were trying to hide. Their breathing was shallow, I could hear their
heart beat. I joys of enhanced senses. But if he were Venatori he too heard me,
knew I was here. I didn't shout, he'd hear me, "Levi you need to come out."

Nothing came in response, but I heard his breath catch, and his heart flutter as
I called his name. I was trained to do this. I was a hunter. I found a veil
wrapping a corner. I smiled. I knew he thought he was safe. I could feel his
breath on the air. I could see the veil shimmer and shake in the patterns, he
was nervous, scared and I didn't blame him. "Levi, come out. I know where you
are. You can't hide from me, you aren't that good. You'll never be that good at
a 4."

I tooka another step closer. I could hear him gasp as I stepped again. "Levi
come on out. You know I know where you are."

He still didn't move I stepped closer. I hated to do it, it would hurt, but I
ripped the veil from Levi's grasp. The pattern crumpled and he collapsed to the
ground gasping for breath. I knelt down and looked at him, "I told you I knew
where you were. You can't hid e from me Levi."

He just gasped for air. "Stand up and let's go."

He tried to run. He stumbled forward, his momentum crashing him into one of the
shelves and toppled it over. I stood up and let the boy think he had gotten
away. "You won't find any way out Levi."

I heard the door open and then a loud off and Levi ran into the air pattern I'd
created at the door to keep anyone in and others out. "I told you Levi, you
aren't going anywhere."

Levi scrambled elsewhere and I followed the sound of his footsteps. "Levi..."

There was no where in the store room to go. I started methodically blocking off
areas I had already passed so he couldn't double back. He'd corner himself
eventually the room was only so big.

I was at the door and there was only a few places to hide. "Come on, Levi come
out. Let's not do this."

"Just go away Nox. Please, he'll kill me!"

"Who will kill you?"

"Just go away."

"I'm sorry. I can't." I didn't want to do this, I didn't want to hurt this kids,
but it was likely I was going to have to.

Levi stepped out of the corner he was hiding in. He was shaking. He was afraid
and I wasn't sure if it was me or the person who'd 'kill' him.

"Please go away." I couldn't do that he knew it. I shook my head. The kid fell
to his knees and started to weep.

"Come on Levi lets go." I picked him up by the arm and had to literally carry
him with the air because he weighed more than I could carry the distance I
needed to go.

I called Emilio. He answered, "Nox."

"Yeah. I got the boy heading to Dae'lin's office."

"I got some good news too, was about to call. I got the guy we are looking for,
sending out an all call with his picture."

Levi started struggling and I tightened the bonds. It was the only thing I could
do as I dragged his body to the conference room.

I finally got to Dae'lin's office and Dae'lin was frowning at me with the boy
tied up with air. "What proof do you have?"

I didn't have any. I only had a hunch and a few things. "You mean other than the
fact that he was hiding. And that he says someone will kill him if he talks to
us?"

Dae'lin sighed, "You know this isn't proof."

I laughed, "Since when did you need proof? I thought we were judge, jury and
executioner." I tried not to spit the words out, but from the expression on
Dae'lin's face she knew how bitter it had tasted in my mouth.

Emilio choose that time to come in, "We don't need proof. But I'd prefer if we
didn't have to kill the boy. Let's get him talking."

I shook my head, "He's not talking."

Emilio nodded, "You know him? See what you can do. Otherwise I'll have to employ
other tactics you might not like son."

I glared at Emilio. This was exactly what I hated about the Venatori. I sighed
and went to do my job. I would talk to Levi.

He was sitting in a chair now wrapped in air and earth that I'd bound him with.
He struggled and the earth bit into his arms. He stopped struggling as hard as
the blood welled along his wrists.

I sat down opposite of him. "Levi. Who would kill you?"

He shook his head, tears started to stream down his cheeks. "I can't."

"You know the charges against you?" I didn't wait for him to answer me. "One
count attempted murder, one count murder and one count accomplice to murder."
Levi paled as I stated the charges that would be held against him.

Levi looked scared, "I didn't know."

"You didn't know you'd be charged when you killed someone? You didn't know you'd
kill someone with the bombs? Did you know your pattern was unstable? That you
did it wrong?"

Levi's turned white. "You forget Levi. I am Cesari. I see what you do, I know
what is possible and I know how to do far more than you can even dream of
doing."

The boy sneered at me and I smiled. "Tell me who is going to hurt you?"

"Why should I tell you anything? Your an arragont prick!"

I laughed. "You just now seeing that?"

There was little to do I sighed. "I'm going to have to let Mr. Vega in. You do
remember him don't you? You killed his wife. I'm sure he has some pretty good
ideas how to make you talk."

I stood up to leave. Levi grabbed my arm as it passed the arm of his chair where
he was tied. "He will kill me if I talk to you."

I nodded, "Levi, what do you think the penalty for murdering one of our own is?"
I didn't wait for him to asnwer. "Death. There will be no trial. There will be
no jury. We have all the proof we need that you killed Dolores Vega. Your hat
you kindly strap to your belt was seen handing her the package. You are cesari
and a crappy one at that. I could kill you now, but we need information. So you
know now, you are dead anyway. Tell or not. Either way it's the same."

I pulled my arm from from Levi's grasp and I started for the door. I was done, I
couldn't do what was needed. Levi shouted, "His name is Abraham Morgan."

Emilio asked over the intercom, "Who is he?"

I knew that answer, "Let me guess, he's the minorem son of Karla Cox. She was
exiled by you and my father. She'd taken up with a human. Mitchel Morgan. They
last reported in 30 years ago."

I walked out of the room. I wanted away from the boy who was a traitor to our
kind.

# The Best Laid Plans

_Tuesday, June 16, 2015 1:10PM_

Emilio came into the conference room and I stopped in the doorway to listen.
"Nox. This boy will help us." Emilio spoke in soft quiet voice that made me
remember the one and only time Dorian had used a voice like that. It had been
the only time I'd ever hurt someone. Dorian had said he was disappointed in me.
I begged and pleaded and assured him I'd never do it again. I'd never hurt
anyone again. I had wanted to threaten Levi and I frowned at myself.

I turned to Emilio. "He'll help. Even if he doesn't want to." I walked out of
the room and paced outside the conference room. I looked down at the floor as I
paced, I needed to regain myself. Too many times since coming home had my
memories overtaken my control.

In front of me I saw a pair of black leather shoes so polished I could almost
see myself in them. I looked up but I already knew who it was. There was only
one person who smelled like that. I smiled at him but it hardly reached my eyes.
His smiled turned to a frown when my eyes met his. "What's wrong?" Dorian asked
me.

I shrugged my shoulders, "Just memories. Coincidence. Too many." I nodded in the
direction, "Your father has an angry voice like you."

Dorian raised an eyebrow at me, "When have I been angry with you?"

I smirked at him. "Only once Dorian. When I hurt Garrett. You told me you were
disappointed in me."

He sighed, "I remember that. I ..."

I smiled and put my hand on Dorian's arm, "No words Dorian. I'm okay. I just
remembered what I promised and what I was thinking about doing to Levi only
moments before your dad came in."

Dorian put his arm around me and I put my head agaisnt his shoulder. "I'm okay."
I took a deep breath and all I could smell the comfort of vanilla and cinamomn
and Dorian. "I met a little boy who does what I do."

Dorian asked softly, "Does what?"

I grinned against his shoulder and stood up straight, "Takes comfort in things
that smell like home and safety." I smiled at Dorian, "I need you to go back up
to the infirmary. Your dad needs you safe." I leaned my head agaist Dorian's
forehead and whispered, "I need you safe."

Dorian nodded, "I will do as you ask. But only because you asked." I swallowed
hard as Dorian pulled me close to him. "But you promise me, you'll be safe."

I kissed Dorian softly, it was just a brush of the lips nothng more even though
my body ached for it, "I will stay as safe as I possibly can."

Dorian nodded, "It's all I ask." He ran his fingers down the right side of my
face from my temple to my chin. I could feel it tigniting things inside me, he
grinned at me like he knew the effect he had on me. Dorian looked at me with a
grin. "You are destroying my carefully laid reputation." He winked at me, "And
I'm letting you."

I caught Dorian's arm before he left, "I don't want to destroy it."

Dorian smiled, "I know. It's why I let you." He put his lips on mine and kissed
me hard. He pulled away breathless, "I need to get up to the infirmary."

I laughed. Dorian saw his father standing in the doorway watching us and he
looked back at me with a grin then headed towards the infirmary.

Emilio smiled at me, "He's never been so open about..."

I grinned at him and put my finger to my lips to silence him. He laughed. "We
will have Levi send a message to this Abraham and meet him at the armory. The
boy is more than cooperative."

I nodded, "Sounds good? Where are we doing this?

Emilio smiled, "The armory. A good enough target he'd meet the boy."

"Okay. We need more than me and you."

Dae'lin was standing in her office doorway and watched. I could see the fear in
her eyes, this whole ordeal was scaring her. She wasn't a hunter. She was just a
glorified paper pusher. I sighed and grabbed Levi by the scruff of his neck and
dragged him out of the conference room in front of me. "Let's go."

He tried to run when I pushed him forward. I tripped him with a small thin line
of air. He fell forward on his face with a grunt. "Levi, when will you learn."

I turned to Emilio, "He may say he's cooperating but he doesn't look like he
is." I pulled him up by the scruff of his neck again. I wanted to threaten him,
to tell him I'd kill him if he tried it again. I pushed him forard again and he
stumbled but he walked this time.

Emilio put his hand on my shoulder and whisperd, "It's alright. We'll take care
of this."

We walked to the armory and Levi sat outside the door. There was a hunter I'd
never met sitting in the stair well, another two hiding in the armory itself and
me and Emilio down the hall. I was the only Magnus. Levi was supposedly on our
side, but no one trusted him.

We heard heavy footsteps coming drow the stairs. I knew the man inside was
probably going to bite it. And when he stepped through the doorway with blood
dripping down the corner of his mouth. He fell forward and a man in a brown
leather jacket stood behind him with a wide grin. "Thanks for the warning kid."

Levi smiled at him. "There are two more in the armory and two around the
corner."

Abraham laughed, "Anyone fun?"

Levi grinned, "Emilio Vega and the Viddens boy - Nox. He's like me. He says I'm
Cesari, or that's what they call us. Peopule who can bend all four elements. He
a half human bastard of Kai Viddens."

"Half human eh?" Abraham raised his voice, "Sounds like that would grate under
the skin of these false heros. Right Nox?"

I sighed, he was trying to target my conflicts. Emilio was watching me. I shook
my head. He yelled again, "My boy. I bet they put a leash on you. Gave you a
handler. Someone to tell you where to go. Who to hunt. Do they tell you why you
hunt? Where it all started?"

The world was spinning. The man was saying things that I'd known, that I'd felt
my whole life. But I didn't beleive it. I knew better. Dae'lin wasn't my handler
she was my boss. But Dae'lin did tell me why I was hunting what I was hunting at
the time. I knew what the Venatori told us about our legacy. I wondered what the
man knew and what he was trying to get under my skin.

I smiled at Emilio and nodded. I was going out. He was going to cover me. I went
out with my hands up. I didn't even have a weapon on me.

"I know enough." I smiled. The bald man ran his hand over the top of his head.

"I can enlighten you to the way." He sounded so arragant. I dispised him. I
hated people who assumed I was unhappy with my life.

"I don't need enlightening. I'm rather happy in my ignorance."

Levi spoke up, "Abe, he's a bender. Don't trust him." I could see the patterns
around Levi shifting. I wove quickly. I waved my hand and Emilio would have my
back. Emilio stepped out of the shadows and had a gun pointed. Everything went
sideways then. Abraham fired his gun. I hadn't even seen he'd had one. Levi's
patterns flew and there was only moments to act. I had a shield of air between
me and everyone else in the blink of an eye. A fireball loosed in the next
second. Emilio's gun fired past me and I wrapped him in air and flung him out of
the bullets.

I blinked away the blur and rubbed my ear from the sound of the gunshots. I had
my back to the scene but all I could hear was the sound of Abraham screaming. I
didn't look, I wove a band of air and I used the sound of his screams to find my
target. I used a pattern of air and sliced his head clean from his body. I
looked up from the ground and was looking at Emilio against the wall, he was
holdhing his shoulder but was otherwise alright. But I asked anyway, "You
alright?"

The senior Vega nodded, "I am. I think my shoulder is dislocated but I'm fine."
The men in the armory poked their heads out their guns seeking a target. "Better
late than never."

I had to laugh, "They did their job, they protected the armory. I had you."

Emilio laughed, "Yeah, but you dislocated my shoulder."

I smiled, "I'm sorry."

Abraham Morgan was dead when I turned around. I saw Levi's body slumped over on
the ground and two weeping holes in his chest. Emilio's target had been true,
take out the most dangerous one. The one that could hurt us the most. Abraham
was minorem. I stood over the burning corpse and doused it with water. The two
from the armory sighed with releif.

Emilio put his arm around my shoulder, "I knew you had him. You could have let
him suffer a little more though."

I looked at the older man and frowned, "I promised your son I would never do
that to anyone again."

Emilio looked at me with sadness in his eyes. "There were rumors back then."

I nodded, "I'd prefer they stay rumors."

Emilio pulled me into a hug, "Of course." He whispered to me, "I think my son
will forgive this act of vengence for his mother and for saving my life."

I shook my head, "I'm sure he will. But that's not the point. His screams
reminded me of that moment in my life. I couldn't let him suffer anymore or I'd
have a panic attack. I didn't give him mercy I was being selfish."

Emilio tightened the hug, "Thank you."

I nodded agasint him chest, "I think we need to get you to the infirmary."

Emilio laughed, "Yes, that is probably a good idea."

# Waiting

_Tuesday, June 16, 2015 2:00PM_

Emilio pulled out his phone and called someone. I heard him tell them to lift
the lockdown and send everyone home. The perps were dead and life was to go back
to normal. They would send cleaners to dispose of the bodies and perpare the
fallen hunter for an honorable funeral.

I walked with Emilio towards the infirmary. He seemed to be in a bit of pain,
"You need assistance?"

Emilio shook his head, "It could have been worse. I don't know what you saved me
from, the fireball or the bullets, but either way I am grateful."

I smiled, "No problem." I noticed Emilio was sliding his leg a little more with
each step. I picked up his arm and wrapped it around my shoulders and helped the
senior Vega, "Let me help you. I'd hate to see you fall down."

Emilio laughed, "I ain't that old son."

I grinned back at him, "As you say, sir." He chuckled at me and we made our way
to the elevator as the lockdown lifted. I braced myself for the short rise to
the infirmary. I was at least distracted from most of it with Emilio's weight on
my shoulders.

He felt me stiffen as we ascended, he chuckled to himself, "You can fight
dragons, and vampires and creatures with lycanthropy but the little itty bitty
elevator ride makes you uncomfortable."

I laughed, when you put it like that it sounded even worse than it felt. "We all
have our issues."

Emilio nodded, "We do at that."

The elevator doors opened into the lobby of the infirmary and Emilio pointed to
the correct location where Kai's family would be waiting for the surgury to be
completed. We didn't make it that far before a nurse stopped in front of us and
frowned, "What happened to him?"

Emilio laughed, "I was thrown against a wall to save my life."

The woman frowned. I smiled my best friendly smile and her frown softened but it
didn't go away, "He has a dislocated shoulder and I think he might have been hit
by a stray bullet in the leg. But I can't say for sure, he's limping a bit."

Emilio looked down, "Yeah and everythings starting to hurt now that the
adrenaline is fading." The nurse called for a wheel chair and I held Emilio as
he nodded down the cooridor. "They are in there, son. Go check on them, and your
father and tell my son I'm fine."

I nodded, "Yes sir." The nurse and I helped Emilio down into the wheel chair and
I watched as he was wheeled the opposit direction. I walked slowly towards the
waiting room. I wasn't part of the family but he was my father and I did care
despite what people might think.

From behind I felt an arm wrap around my waist and hand me a styrofoam cup full
of what smelled like burnt coffee. I leaned into Dorian's embrace and took the
coffee and a sip before I turned to smile at him. "You father is being seen now,
he's fine. Though I think I dislocated his shoulder when I threw him to safety."

"Threw him?" Dorian asked with curiousity.

"Everything happened so fast there was little time to do much else. How's Kai?"
I asked. We had stopped just outside the waiting room near a wall out of the
way.

Dorian shrugged, "Still in surgery." He cocked his head to the side before, "Do
you want me to stay?"

I looked into the waiting room and saw people with whom I really didn't know.
They were family but they weren't too. I nodded my head, "Yes, please. But I
have to go do something first. I promised someone. You can come with."

Dorian nodded, and we headed back down to the boys dorms. Mr. Lance was herding
boys through doors. He sighed with releif at me. "You are right they won't open
the door."

I nodded, "That's why I'm here. I'll take care of it." I headed towards the room
that I'd told them to stay. I stood before the orange door and tried my hardest
not to freak out over it. I felt Dorian's hand at the small of my back. I smiled
at him and then knocked on the door. "Go away." A small voice yelled from the
other side.

"It's me, you can come out now. It's safe. The bad men are all gone."

I heard small voices talking and then I heard the door unlock and one golden eye
opened the door and peeked through. He smiled and opened the door fully and
tossed himself at me. I managed to grab him before he fell to the floor. The
other three boys tumbled after him and I fell to the floor in a heap of boys. I
grinned I had not expect all of them to fling themselves at me, but there it
was.

I sat up and the boys were giggling. "Mr. Lance will take care of you now. Okay.
I need you to listen to him."

They all nodded as Mr. Lance walked into the double doors that had separated the
hall from the common area. "Good, come along boys. We've got some cleaning to
do."

They scrambled up after Mr. Lance and he nodded in my direction. Dorian offered
me a hand up which I gratefully took. He grinned at me, "I like watching you in
your element."

I had a feeling I knew what he meant but I just grinned at him and let it go. I
had to go see my so-called family now. Dorian saw the hesitation in my eyes and
he wrapped his arm around my waist and guided me through the halls and back to
the Infirmary. I looked inside and I truly wanted to leave, but I wanted to know
how my fater was doing, and that required waiting on the doctors to return, so I
went in.

Iris looked up with grief and worry in her eyes. She smiled at me and spoke
softly, "Thank you for catching the man who did this."

I nodded, "I didn't do it alone. But I'm glad we got him too."

She smiled and turned back to her family, she was holding her daughters hand and
her husband stood near by with a look that said he wanted to be elsewhere.

Dorian and I sat down in a corner away from the rest of them. I felt completely
out of place in their family space they'd occupied. There were kids sprawled out
on the floor. Two were coloring and a third was playing with several matchbox
cars. I grinned as I watched him play.

A rather large man stood in front of me. I looked up to find my oldest half
brother standing above me considering what to say. His eyes were rimmed in red
and his eyes were puffy. He'd been crying recently. I waved my hand to the chair
and he sat down next to me without prompting, which I was grateful for he was
making me nervous. I glanced at him from my seat and he just sat there. I
smiled, "You're welcome. He didn't go quietly."

Adam smirked. "I'm glad."

We sat in silence, the children were the only ones chattering with one another.
Dorian sat with his leg pressed against mine and Adam at my other side, it was
oddly comforting to be accepted.

A doctor stepped into the room and Iris and Adam both stood up and they walked
over to him. I could have eavesdropped had I wanted to, instead I watched my
half-sister's expression. The relief flooded her face and I knew Kai would be
fine. She smiled and her and Adam shared a quick hug before they returned to
their families. Adam came back and sat down next to me and smiled, "He'll be
alright."

I grinned, "He's too stubborn to let a little stabbing stop him."

Adam laughed, "That is the truth."

The mood in the room had lightened. Everyone was feeling slightly better. Iris
smiled, "Father is going to be fine, if he wakes up. We all know he can't stand
to be bed ridden, he'll be up and attem before no time."

Iris looked to her husband and he was already ushering their children out the
door. She came and sat down next to Adam. Marius was already out the door, "I'm
gonna grab some grub."

Iris smiled, "Go home. Get some rest, no need for all of us to stay here and
wait."

I nodded, "You sure?"

She nodded, "Yeah, he's gonna be fine. You've done enough for Father now. Go get
some sleep." Iris reached acrossed her brother's lap and patted my knee. "Eat.
Come back tomorrow. Don't be a stranger."

I nodded. Dorian took my hand and I stood next to him, Adam frowned at the
gesture but Iris smiled as Dorian spoke, "He won't."

"I'll see you tomorrow." I nodded, "Both of you."

Dorian wrapped his arm around my waist when we made it out of the waiting room
door. "Let's go have an early dinner."

I laughed, "I didn't have time to get anything."

Dorian grinned, "Don't worry about it, we'll figure something out."

We walked in silence the rest of the way. Dorian's arm guiding me. We took the
elevator up to Dorian's room. Dorian let me have my back to the lobby and he
stood in front of me. He smiled and watched my face as we rode the elevator. My
body tensed as we started rising, his hand rubbing small circles at the small of
my back. I leaned into his chest and let him comfort me. He chuckled softly,
"The first time you did that I was at a loss for words. I didn't know what to
do."

I pulled back and looked at him with a grin. "You did everything I needed you
to."

"It's a little ironic don't you think?" He asked.

I shrugged, "Maybe, but I don't want to think about it. I like where this is
going."

Dorian nodded, "I do too." The doors opened and Dorian turned around and held my
hand the whole way to his room. There was no one between here and there, but I
was surprised at all the open displays. I had never seen Dorian with anyone so
openly before. His father hadn't either from what he'd said earlier.

Dorian unlocked the door to his rooms and let me in before he shut the door
behind him. I still felt like I didn't want to touch anything. Everything was
perfect in here. Almost museum quality. Dorian left me standing again in his
door way as he started opening and closing cabinets. I grinned and walked over
to the bar and sat down in the blood red swivle chair and gave it a spin before
catching myself on the edge of the bar.

I looked up and saw Dorian grinning at me. I asked, "What are you looking for?"

Dorian blushed slightly, "Coffee. I didn't figure you'd want wine."

I laughed, "Cupboard by the fridge, second shelf. I put it back where I found
it."

Dorian nodded, "I don't make coffee at home often. Usually get it on the go."

I nodded, "I know."

He gave me a fake glare as he walked around the bar and stood next to my chair
and turned me to face him, stepping between my legs. "If you think you know my
kitchen so well, you find it." He grinned at me.

I smiled up at him and stood up. My body pressed against his because he didn't
move to let me stand. I could feel the heat of his body through my clothes and I
licked my lips. "I don't mind if I do."

Dorian chuckled and stepped aside, letting me walke around the bar to make
coffee. When I turned around Dorian was sitting in the seat I'd vacated only
