kitchen that he hardly used.

"You hungry?" I asked him.

He nodded, "I am. Are you? I'm sure you've not eaten since breakfast."

I laughed, "At least I ate breakfast. But yes I'm fanished."

Dorian laughed, "I think there is food in the fridge."

I opened it expecting to find nothing really but I was wrong, there was a
package of what I could only assume were stake and in the vegetable drawers were
actual vegetables. I grinned at them as I pulled everything out. Dorian smiled,
"I had my assistant run an errand for me. She said she knew exactly what to
buy."

I nodded, "You had Claudia buy dinner for you?"

"I didn't think you'd have time. And it insured that you'd actually cook for me
again." Dorian chuckled.

I grined and walked around the bar and wrapped my arms around his neck from
behind and kissed his neck, "You are too thoughtful."

Dorian spun around in my arms and wrapped his arms around my back and fished out
my phone. I laughed, "You want me to dance around too eh?"

Dorian only smiled at me as he turned back around to flip through my phone and
the playlists on it.

I walked around the bar and started to prepare dinner. I washed the vegetables
before turning around to use the bar and chop them so I could throw them in the
oven. Dorian continued to flip through the music on my phone. He was either not
finding what he wanted or he was lost somewhere on it. I couldn't tell but I
smiled as I watched him as I methodically cut the carrots and squash his
assitant had bought. There was even some corn, I hated corn on the cob. Not the
food itself but prepping it always sucked. All those silk hairs drove me crazy.

My phone rang and Dorian nearly dropped my phone on the bar. He looked up at me
and I held up my hands they were full of debris from the corn, he swipped it,
"Nox's phone."

He grinned, "His hands are busy at the moment I can put you on speaker."

Dorian set the phone down and Stella's name sat at the top. "You are on speaker
now."

Stella's sweet voice answered, "Nox?"

"Yeah I'm here." I continued chopping vegetables

"Who answered your phone? I recognize the voice but can't place it."

Dorian chuckled to himself. "That was Dorian - my friend who sent the wine."

Dorian's face turned a slight shade of rose, he hadn't realized I knew he'd sent
it. "As in Dorian Vega?"

I laughed, "Yes ma'am, one and the same."

"How do you know him?"

Dorian was watching my face. "I've known him my whole life for the most part
anyway."

"I thought...Wait you are one of these Venatori?" She was slowly peicing things
together.

I nodded despite the fact that she co uldn't see me. "Yes and no. I'm half
Venatori. I'm more like Aidan. My mother was human, my fahter Veantori."

"And you are what screwing Dorian?"

I laughed, "Well I haven't screwed him yet, if you must know." Dorian blushed
furiously but he remained quiet.

"Did you know he's my ex?" She sounded angry.

"I didn't know when we met. Or when I came over for dinner. Or when you called
me to tell me you had gotten the job. I found out last night after your meeting
with Dorian."

Stella sighed, "He never said anything when I mentioned meeting you. He's
Aidan's father Nox."

"I know. It explains a little."

"How so?"

"It explains why I liked him. Why I was willing to let a strange kid climb all
over me."

"I don't understand." She sounded confused.

I sighed, "Dorian has always been a kind of safety net for me. He was there
after the first time I flew, when I came here. He was there after every single
test and every single thing that went good or wrong with my life. Always there
when I needed to be caught. Your son, despite my recognition of it, reminded me
very much of his father."

"When were you going to tell me you knew this?"

I laughed. "I told you the first chance I got."

She sighed, "I asked."

This was going to go badly either way I looked at it. "Stella. I'm not going to
agrue about this. You are a potential friend, nothing more, by your own
admission. I like Dorian. He's not going anywhere. Call me when you get back to
New York, or when you know exactly your plans. I'll help you move if you need me
to. But Dorian - he's not going anywhere. I need to go. I'm in the middle of
cooking dinner for me and my date and I'd like to finish it off please. Call. Or
don't. You make your choice. I'm with your ex it's not going to change."

Stella hung up. She hadn't even said anything. I sighed, "I don't suppose that
went well. I'm sorry."

Dorian frowned, "I'm sorry. I think this has been a giant mess no matter how you
look at it."

"Nothing either of us could have done differently."

Dorian laughed, "I suppose not. Though I could not have slept with her."

I grinned, "And what fun would that be."

I put the vegetables on a cooking sheet and poured some olive oil and threw on
some herbs and spices and put them in the oven. I started the steaks as Dorian
changed the topic to the music on my phone. He hadn't been lost. He'd said there
is a lot to learn about a person by what they had on their playlist. He had
gotten involved in it until the phone rang. It was then that I learned Dorian
had gone to college for a phscyology degree. It made sense. It also made me
wonder how he had the time to do that and his job in the Venatori. But he had.

We chatted while I finished up the steaks and the vegetables roasted in the
oven. Dorian gave a loud sniff and explaimed, "I don't think my kitchen has ever
smelled so divine."

I laughed, I refrained from my smart as comment about how I was in the kitchen.
I turned to Dorian and he had this look that said he was waiting for me to say
something. I laughed. As I turned back to plate the steaks and let them rest a
few minutes.

Dorian glanced at me with a grin, "I'm going to go change into something more
comfortable."

I grinned at him, my imagination could run wild with a statement like that, and
if a woman had told me that I would have expected to have her come out in
lengerie that left nothing to the imagination, but Dorian was not a woman and I
doubted that was what he meant. He was wearing a suit and tie and had been for

# Father

_Tuesday, June 17, 2015 7:00AM_

# Epilogue

_Tuesday, June 17, 2015 9:15AM_

There was something about having family that seemed to make things better. And
knowing that family was more than just blood made it better. Kai was my father,
that made all the rest of the Viddens family. But really I think it was the
Vegas that had shown me more love in the past three days than my own. And that
probably had a lot to do with me pushing people away. I was going to have a lot
to talk about with Margo come next Monday. I was going to have to start jotting
these things down so I don't forget.

But family wasn't everything on my mind as I wandered the halls of the compound
I had grown up in. There was what Abraham had said, and what I'd already felt.
Why I didn't kill the creatures I hunted unless my life depended on it. Or
others did. They always died of course, but it wasn't by my hand. I wasn't being
judge jury and executioner. I let someone else do that dirty work. I hunted. And
I was beginning to think that maybe I wasn't the best person for the job.

I'd sat down with Levi and I'd gotten through to him. Drake had taken to me with
ease as had Aidan without me ever really trying. I wanted to be around for my
kids. I was going to have kids. I'm 22 and here I am thinking that kids are in
my near future. There is no potential Ms. Sétana to share that joy with. Though
there are possiblities just not biological in means.

I found it odd considering a future with someone. But that was the train of
thought that Dorian pulled at. More. Did I really want more? To be with this man
who'd been a guiding light? Was it just my childhood dreams living through him?
I don't know and right now I didn't care.

I pondered all these things as I wandered the compound. I found myself opening
the door to the roof. The one place when I was young where the world stopped
being about everything else and became about me. I knew my fears. I knew my
strengths. And this fear wouldn't be my weakness. I still quake at the thought
of looking over the edge, but I do it anyway. My body doesn't shut down when I
ride the elevator anymore. I don't lose myself in my fears. I learned to
concquer them.

And though I've slept better in the past two nights than I have in forever, I
know I'm not better. I know I'll dream of Garret again. I know hi'll weild whips
of air and earth and fling tham at my bare skin again. The mere thought of it
send a cold chill down my spine. But I didn't have to face this alone anymore.
I'd told the right people. I could only hope that it stayed there. I didn't want
people to pity me to see the broken kid that I am inside. I'm not that person.

I sat down against the ledge of the roof and opened the envelope. Inside was a
multi page document, and a small slip of paper that bore the sloppy hand writing
of I assumed my father.

I read the letter first.

****

Nox,

I know I've made some presumptions. It is not to dictate your life. Only to make
your children's life better than your own. I know you and Dorian are only in the
beginnings of whatever relationship the two of you forsee. I do not expect you
to love Dorian. This is a union of betterment. A part of the breeding program.

You know the damange of no parents. A single parent is much the same. As me
about my childhood one day and I'll give you more insights into how we are the
same. Of all my children you remind me too much of the past I fought to never
give my children. And yet one slipped through my fingers. I cannot forgive
myself that.

A signle parent is hard. I know you cannot be both favored and hated at the same
time, one needs to be present for either side, even if you are both hated or
favored at the same time. A shared burden. I don't mean to proclude other
relationships. You and Dorian can choose to be only friends for this agreement
to remain intact but both raising the children. Being both mother and father.
Being what the child's other parent cannot be for whatever reasons.

I know you will be a better parent than yours were to you. But know I will be
the best grandfather I can be to your children, to make up for the lack of being
there for you as a child.

Your Father, Kai.

****

There were always stories, always reasons why a person is the way they are. One
day, someday soon, I hoped maybe I'd find out the reasons my father had used
favors to get whatever he wanted in on this document. I could only guess at the
measures he'd taken to insure my children didn't have a life like I did, or he
did. It was a difficult concept to understand but I knew he had my best
interests at heart I would listen with an open mind. I wasn't going to like
being forced into whatever this was, but betterment of my children and
apparently Dorian's I would do anything to insure their safety above my own.

I read the document enclosed. It had started off as I had expected. Dae'lin and
I had discussed most of it. The only difference being that my children would not
be sterlized no matter their status as Venatori minorem. They would become
Scrin. The fact that I was cesari must have waved their hands in that. They were
willing to accept my limitations to gain more cesari. I could handle that. I was
grateful for it.

But the document went on to add an additional woman to my required list of women
to breed with. I felt like they were studding me out until I read the reasons
for the inclusion. I was releiving Dorian from his duties as Venatori. I could
do the man that favor. I couldn't imagine having to assume a role I had not
enjoyed. Actually I could, and I had on many occasions, I didn't wish it on
anyone.

Dorian would not be left out of the heirs or pushing forward his line, he just
didn't have to with the woman they'd originally chosen for him. My father had
found a donor to provide an egg and a surrogate mother to provide the incubation
of an heir through IVF. It was unheard of unless a couple was infertile, this
was the first for a man who enjoyed the company of men. It was a large step
forward.

And it was the final clause that finally made my father's letter make sense.
Dorian and I were to be legally unionized. We would legally hold rights together
as a married couple. It may not be legal in the United States, but among the
Venatori with Venatori lawyers and judges and the like, it would be law. The
council deemed it so, thus it was law. It was the way the Venatori worked. And
it was the part that was the hardest to accept. Not that I didn't want to be
with Dorian, it's the thought that I was being forced into this relationship
regardless of our own feelings. The thought that the Venatori could control my
life to that degree. It was exactly what I hated about this life. Yet I couldn't
do anything to change it.

I knew I would accept. I knew that in the end I'd end up hurting Dorian over
this. I knew this. I knew my mind. I knew my heart. And what killed me in that
moment was that I didn't want to be me.

There was too much, and I needed to escape. So I did the only thing I knew how
to do. I jumped. I wove wings of air and catapulted myself over the ledge like a
pole vaulter and I fell to the ground. I could do it in my sleep, I softened the
earth, veiled my descent and I listened to the air rush past my ears, the blood
coursing through my veins as I fell. I let everything go in those 8 seconds it
took gravity to bring me rushing to the ground. It was my time. There were no
monsters to hunt, no contracts to sign. These were my 8 seconds, and no one
could take them from me.

****

The view from my glass office atop the Bank of America building was gorgious
this time of day. The sun was behind me and I had a perfect view of the New York
Skyline. I was lost in thought of the recent merger I as contimplating when the
sudden decent of a body broke the sight line. I followed the body down, until it
became nothing but a speck on the grassy ground beneath. The kids usually only
jumped at night, when they had less of a chance of getting caught. At least that
was how it had been for the past few years. Rumor had it that their leader had
returned and he was the only one capable of jumping from the height unassisted.
He was the creator of the stupid stunt, he used to do it alone or with one other
boy, until the rest of the benders found out. Now just above my office nearly
every night was a party of children who flung themselves from the rooftops,
bending and catching the currents just right so that they land unscathed.
Children in my time didn't do stupid things - even when they knew they could not
die. These mere mortals were flinging themselves from the heights and they
didn't even realize the peril their lives were in.

The Venatori were careaning on the edge of their very own destruction and the
children were leading the way. It had always been the way of their kind. Even my
dead race had done the same, guiding their lives by a stict structure until they
found yet another reason to relent. The hunters had become too powerful, they
ruled the world and yet the world did not know it was being ruled by them. It
wasn't right. There had to be checks and balances, as there was anything in
life. A dragon who stole should be allowed to keep it's standard of living they
were after all here first. But a dragon who steals too much, yes, a check, but
immediate death? The Venatori were going too far. Death was not the only answer.

I intended to right the wrong, sadly every wrong had its champions as well and
thus far those champions were picking at the carefully tuned fabric of my plan.
I needed to restore those threads before the Venatori completely destroy it. It
was only a matter of time before I found the one I was looking for, the one whom
I saw in my visions. I dreamt about it nightly. I would know the vision when it
happened. I felt it growing close. I knew it was near. The time of the Venatori
was closing and I would have the control this time.
